Admit rejects a pod if its not safe to admit for node stability.\n146: func (m *managerImpl) Admit(attrs *lifecycle.PodAdmitAttributes) lifecycle.PodAdmitResult {\n147: \tm.RLock()\n148: \tdefer m.RUnlock()\n149: \n150: \tctx := context.Background()\n151: \tlogger := klog.FromContext(ctx)\n152: \n153: \tif len(m.nodeConditions) == 0 {\n154: \t\treturn lifecycle.PodAdmitResult{Admit: the control loop to observe and response to low compute resources.\n188: func (m *managerImpl) Start(ctx context.Context, diskInfoProvider DiskInfoProvider, podFunc ActivePodsFunc, podCleanedUpFunc PodCleanedUpFunc, monitoringInterval time.Duration) {\n189: \tlogger := klog.FromContext(ctx)\n190: \tthresholdHandler := func(message string) {\n191: \t\tlogger.Info(message)\n192: \t\t_, _ = m.synchronize(ctx, diskInfoProvider, podFunc)\n193: \t}\n194: \tlogger.Info(\"Eviction manager: starting control loop\")\n195: \tif m.config.KernelMemcgNotification || runtime.GOOS == \"windows\" {\n196: \t\tfor _, threshold := range m.config.Thresholds {\n197: \t\t\tif threshold.Signal == evictionapi.SignalMemoryAvailable || threshold.Signal == evictionapi.SignalAllocatableMemoryAvailable hasNodeCondition(m.nodeConditions, v1.NodeMemoryPressure)\n230: }\n231: \n232: // IsUnderDiskPressure returns true if the node is under disk pressure.\n233: func (m *managerImpl) IsUnderDiskPressure() \n246: // synchronize is the main control loop that enforces eviction thresholds.\n247: // Returns the pod that was killed, or nil if no pod was killed.\n248: func (m *managerImpl) synchronize(ctx context.Context, diskInfoProvider DiskInfoProvider, podFunc ActivePodsFunc) ([]*v1.Pod, error) {\n249: \tlogger := klog.FromContext(ctx)\n250: \t// if we have nothing to do, just return\n251: \tthresholds := m.config.Thresholds\n252: \tif len(thresholds) == 0 && !m.localStorageCapacityIsolation {\n253: \t\treturn nil, nil\n254: \t}\n255: \n256: \tlogger.V(3).Info(\"Eviction manager: synchronize housekeeping\")\n257: \t// build the ranking functions (if not yet known)\n258: \t// TODO: have a function in cadvisor that lets us know if global housekeeping has completed\n259: \tif m.dedicatedImageFs == nil {\n260: \t\thasImageFs, imageFsErr := diskInfoProvider.HasDedicatedImageFs(ctx)\n261: \t\tif imageFsErr != nil {\n262: \t\t\t// TODO: This should be refactored to log an error and retry the HasDedicatedImageFs\n263: \t\t\t// If we have a transient error this will never be retried and we will not set eviction signals\n264: \t\t\tlogger.Error(imageFsErr, \"Eviction manager: failed to get HasDedicatedImageFs\")\n265: \t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"eviction manager: failed to get HasDedicatedImageFs: %w\", imageFsErr)\n266: \t\t}\n267: \t\tm.dedicatedImageFs = &hasImageFs\n268: \t\tsplitContainerImageFs, splitErr := diskInfoProvider.HasDedicatedContainerFs(ctx)\n269: \t\tif splitErr != nil {\n270: \t\t\t// A common error case is when there is no split filesystem\n271: \t\t\t// there is an error finding the split filesystem label and we want to ignore these errors\n272: \t\t\tlogger.Error(splitErr, \"eviction manager: failed to check if we have separate container filesystem. Ignoring.\")\n273: \t\t}\n274: \n275: \t\t// If we are a split filesystem but the feature is turned off\n276: \t\t// we should return an error.\n277: \t\t// This is a bad state.\n278: \t\tif !utilfeature.DefaultFeatureGate.Enabled(features.KubeletSeparateDiskGC) && splitContainerImageFs {\n279: \t\t\tsplitDiskError := fmt.Errorf(\"KubeletSeparateDiskGC is turned off but we still have a split filesystem\")\n280: \t\t\treturn nil, splitDiskError\n281: \t\t}\n282: \t\tthresholds, err := UpdateContainerFsThresholds(m.config.Thresholds, hasImageFs, splitContainerImageFs)\n283: \t\tm.config.Thresholds = thresholds\n284: \t\tif err != nil {\n285: \t\t\tlogger.Error(err, \"eviction manager: found conflicting containerfs eviction. Ignoring.\")\n286: \t\t}\n287: \t\tm.splitContainerImageFs = &splitContainerImageFs\n288: \t\tm.signalToRankFunc = buildSignalToRankFunc(hasImageFs, splitContainerImageFs)\n289: \t\tm.signalToNodeReclaimFuncs = buildSignalToNodeReclaimFuncs(m.imageGC, m.containerGC, hasImageFs, splitContainerImageFs)\n290: \t}\n291: \n292: \tlogger.V(3).Info(\"FileSystem detection\", \"DedicatedImageFs\", m.dedicatedImageFs, \"SplitImageFs\", m.splitContainerImageFs)\n293: \tactivePods := podFunc()\n294: \tupdateStats := true\n295: \tsummary, err := m.summaryProvider.Get(ctx, updateStats)\n296: \tif err != nil {\n297: \t\tlogger.Error(err, \"Eviction manager: failed to get summary stats\")\n298: \t\treturn nil, nil\n299: \t}\n300: \n301: \tif m.clock.Since(m.thresholdsLastUpdated) > notifierRefreshInterval {\n302: \t\tm.thresholdsLastUpdated = m.clock.Now()\n303: \t\tfor _, notifier := range m.thresholdNotifiers {\n304: \t\t\tif err := notifier.UpdateThreshold(ctx, summary); err != nil {\n305: \t\t\t\tlogger.Info(\"Eviction manager: failed to update notifier\", \"notifier\", notifier.Description(), \"err\", err)\n306: \t\t\t}\n307: \t\t}\n308: \t}\n309: \n310: \t// make observations and get a function to derive pod usage stats relative to those observations.\n311: \tobservations, statsFunc := makeSignalObservations(logger, summary)\n312: \tdebugLogObservations(logger, \"observations\", observations)\n313: \n314: \t// determine the set of thresholds met independent of grace period\n315: \tthresholds = thresholdsMet(logger, thresholds, observations, false)\n316: \tdebugLogThresholdsWithObservation(logger, \"thresholds - ignoring grace period\", thresholds, observations)\n317: \n318: \t// determine the set of thresholds previously met that have not yet satisfied the associated min-reclaim\n319: \tif len(m.thresholdsMet) > 0 {\n320: \t\tthresholdsNotYetResolved := thresholdsMet(logger, m.thresholdsMet, observations, true)\n321: \t\tthresholds = mergeThresholds(thresholds, thresholdsNotYetResolved)\n322: \t}\n323: \tdebugLogThresholdsWithObservation(logger, \"thresholds - reclaim not satisfied\", thresholds, observations)\n324: \n325: \t// track when a threshold was first observed\n326: \tnow := m.clock.Now()\n327: \tthresholdsFirstObservedAt := thresholdsFirstObservedAt(thresholds, m.thresholdsFirstObservedAt, now)\n328: \n329: \t// the set of node conditions that are triggered by currently observed thresholds\n330: \tnodeConditions := nodeConditions(thresholds)\n331: \tif len(nodeConditions) > 0 {\n332: \t\tlogger.V(3).Info(\"Eviction manager: node conditions - observed\", \"nodeCondition\", nodeConditions)\n333: \t}\n334: \n335: \t// track when a node condition was last observed\n336: \tnodeConditionsLastObservedAt := nodeConditionsLastObservedAt(nodeConditions, m.nodeConditionsLastObservedAt, now)\n337: \n338: \t// node conditions report true if it has been observed within the transition period window\n339: \tnodeConditions = nodeConditionsObservedSince(nodeConditionsLastObservedAt, m.config.PressureTransitionPeriod, now)\n340: \tif len(nodeConditions) > 0 {\n341: \t\tlogger.V(3).Info(\"Eviction manager: node conditions - transition period not met\", \"nodeCondition\", nodeConditions)\n342: \t}\n343: \n344: \t// determine the set of thresholds we need to drive eviction behavior (i.e. all grace periods are met)\n345: \tthresholds = thresholdsMetGracePeriod(logger, thresholdsFirstObservedAt, now)\n346: \tdebugLogThresholdsWithObservation(logger, \"thresholds - grace periods satisfied\", thresholds, observations)\n347: \n348: \t// update internal state\n349: \tm.Lock()\n350: \tm.nodeConditions = nodeConditions\n351: \tm.thresholdsFirstObservedAt = thresholdsFirstObservedAt\n352: \tm.nodeConditionsLastObservedAt = nodeConditionsLastObservedAt\n353: \tm.thresholdsMet = thresholds\n354: \n355: \t// determine the set of thresholds whose stats have been updated since the last sync\n356: \tthresholds = thresholdsUpdatedStats(logger, thresholds, observations, m.lastObservations)\n357: \tdebugLogThresholdsWithObservation(logger, \"thresholds - updated stats\", thresholds, observations)\n358: \n359: \tm.lastObservations = observations\n360: \tm.Unlock()\n361: \n362: \t// evict pods if there is a resource usage violation from local volume temporary storage\n363: \t// If eviction happens in localStorageEviction function, skip the rest of eviction action\n364: \tif m.localStorageCapacityIsolation {\n365: \t\tif evictedPods := m.localStorageEviction(logger, activePods, statsFunc); len(evictedPods) > 0 {\n366: \t\t\treturn evictedPods, nil\n367: \t\t}\n368: \t}\n369: \n370: \tif len(thresholds) == 0 {\n371: \t\tlogger.V(3).Info(\"Eviction manager: no resources are starved\")\n372: \t\treturn nil, nil\n373: \t}\n374: \n375: \t// rank the thresholds by eviction priority\n376: \tsort.Sort(byEvictionPriority(thresholds))\n377: \tthresholdToReclaim, resourceToReclaim, foundAny := getReclaimableThreshold(logger, thresholds)\n378: \tif !foundAny {\n379: \t\treturn nil, nil\n380: \t}\n381: \tlogger.Info(\"Eviction manager: attempting to reclaim\", \"resourceName\", resourceToReclaim)\n382: \n383: \t// record an event about the resources we are now attempting to reclaim via eviction\n384: \tm.recorder.Eventf(m.nodeRef, v1.EventTypeWarning, \"EvictionThresholdMet\", \"Attempting to reclaim %s\", resourceToReclaim)\n385: \n386: \t// check if there are node-level resources we can reclaim to reduce pressure before evicting end-user pods.\n387: \tif m.reclaimNodeLevelResources(ctx, thresholdToReclaim.Signal, resourceToReclaim) {\n388: \t\tlogger.Info(\"Eviction manager: able to reduce resource pressure without evicting pods.\", \"resourceName\", resourceToReclaim)\n389: \t\treturn nil, nil\n390: \t}\n391: \n392: \tlogger.Info(\"Eviction manager: must evict pod(s) to reclaim\", \"resourceName\", resourceToReclaim)\n393: \n394: \t// rank the pods for eviction\n395: \trank, ok := m.signalToRankFunc[thresholdToReclaim.Signal]\n396: \tif !ok {\n397: \t\tlogger.Error(nil, \"Eviction manager: no ranking function for signal\", \"threshold\", thresholdToReclaim.Signal)\n398: \t\treturn nil, nil\n399: \t}\n400: \n401: \t// the only candidates viable for eviction are those pods that had anything running.\n402: \tif len(activePods) == 0 {\n403: \t\tlogger.Error(nil, \"Eviction manager: eviction thresholds have been met, but no pods are active to evict\")\n404: \t\treturn nil, nil\n405: \t}\n406: \n407: \t// rank the running pods for eviction for the specified resource\n408: \trank(activePods, statsFunc)\n409: \n410: \tlogger.Info(\"Eviction manager: pods ranked for eviction\", \"pods\", klog.KObjSlice(activePods))\n411: \n412: \t//record age of metrics for met thresholds that we are using for evictions.\n413: \tfor _, t := range thresholds {\n414: \t\ttimeObserved := observations[t.Signal].time\n415: \t\tif !timeObserved.IsZero() {\n416: \t\t\tmetrics.EvictionStatsAge.WithLabelValues(string(t.Signal)).Observe(metrics.SinceInSeconds(timeObserved.Time))\n417: \t\t}\n418: \t}\n419: \n420: \t// we kill at most a single pod during each eviction interval\n421: \tfor i := range activePods {\n422: \t\tpod := activePods[i]\n423: \t\tgracePeriodOverride := int64(immediateEvictionGracePeriodSeconds)\n424: \t\tif !isHardEvictionThreshold(thresholdToReclaim) {\n425: \t\t\tgracePeriodOverride = m.config.MaxPodGracePeriodSeconds\n426: \t\t\tif pod.Spec.TerminationGracePeriodSeconds != nil {\n427: \t\t\t\tgracePeriodOverride = min(m.config.MaxPodGracePeriodSeconds, *pod.Spec.TerminationGracePeriodSeconds)\n428: \t\t\t}\n429: \t\t}\n430: \n431: \t\tmessage, annotations := evictionMessage(resourceToReclaim, pod, statsFunc, thresholds, observations)\n432: \t\tcondition := &v1.PodCondition{\n433: \t\t\tType:               v1.DisruptionTarget,\n434: \t\t\tObservedGeneration: pod.Generation,\n435: \t\t\tStatus:             v1.ConditionTrue,\n436: \t\t\tReason:             v1.PodReasonTerminationByKubelet,\n437: \t\t\tMessage:            message,\n438: \t\t}\n439: \t\tif m.evictPod(logger, pod, gracePeriodOverride, message, annotations, condition) {\n440: \t\t\tmetrics.Evictions.WithLabelValues(string(thresholdToReclaim.Signal)).Inc()\n441: \t\t\treturn []*v1.Pod{pod}, nil\n442: \t\t}\n443: \t}\n444: \tlogger.Info(\"Eviction manager: unable to evict any pods from the node\")\n445: \treturn nil, nil\n446: }\n447: \n448: func (m *managerImpl) waitForPodsCleanup(logger klog.Logger, podCleanedUpFunc PodCleanedUpFunc, pods []*v1.Pod) {\n449: \ttimeout := m.clock.NewTimer(podCleanupTimeout)\n450: \tdefer timeout.Stop()\n451: \tticker := m.clock.NewTicker(podCleanupPollFreq)\n452: \tdefer ticker.Stop()\n453: \tfor {\n454: \t\tselect {\n455: \t\tcase <-timeout.C():\n456: \t\t\tlogger.Info(\"Eviction manager: timed out waiting for pods to be cleaned up\", \"pods\", klog.KObjSlice(pods))\n457: \t\t\treturn\n458: \t\tcase <-ticker.C():\n459: \t\t\tfor i, pod := range pods {\n460: \t\t\t\tif !podCleanedUpFunc(pod) {\n461: \t\t\t\t\tbreak\n462: \t\t\t\t}\n463: \t\t\t\tif i == len(pods)-1 {\n464: \t\t\t\t\tlogger.Info(\"Eviction manager: pods successfully cleaned up\", \"pods\", klog.KObjSlice(pods))\n465: \t\t\t\t\treturn\n466: \t\t\t\t}\n467: \t\t\t}\n468: \t\t}\n469: \t}\n470: }\n471: \n472: // reclaimNodeLevelResources attempts to reclaim node level resources.  returns true if thresholds were satisfied and no pod eviction is required.\n473: func (m *managerImpl) reclaimNodeLevelResources(ctx context.Context, signalToReclaim evictionapi.Signal, resourceToReclaim v1.ResourceName) bool {\n474: \tlogger := klog.FromContext(ctx)\n475: \tnodeReclaimFuncs := m.signalToNodeReclaimFuncs[signalToReclaim]\n476: \tfor _, nodeReclaimFunc := range nodeReclaimFuncs {\n477: \t\t// attempt to reclaim the pressured resource.\n478: \t\tif err := nodeReclaimFunc(ctx); err != nil {\n479: \t\t\tlogger.Info(\"Eviction manager:
